Record: SCPT "tr_m4_andoth_almalexiashrine_sc" Flags:0x0000 ()
  SCHD: ID:TR_m4_Andoth_AlmalexiaShrine_sc  Num_Shorts:3  Num_Longs:0  Num_Floats:0  Data_Size:1079  Local_Var_Size:28
  SCVR: Script_Variables: questionState,button,doOnce
  SCDT: Bytecode: (compiled script code)
  SCTX: Script_Text:
Begin TR_m4_Andoth_AlmalexiaShrine_sc

; Script on Activator TR_m4_Andoth_AlmalexiaShrine.
; This is the Shrine of Almalexia's Fury in Andothren, one of the Temple pilgrimage shrines.

short questionState
short button
short doOnce

if ( OnActivate == 1 )
	Set questionState to 1
	Return
endif

if ( questionState == 0 )
	Return
endif

if ( questionState == 1 )

	if ( Player->GetItemCount "ingred_frost_salts_01" > 0 )
		MessageBox "Would you like to donate Frost Salts and ask for a blessing?" "Yes" "No"
		Set questionState to 2
		Return
	endif

	if ( Player->GetItemCount "T_IngMine_IceCrystal_01" > 0 )
		MessageBox "Would you like to donate an Ice Crystal and ask for a blessing?" "Yes" "No"
		Set questionState to 2
		Return
	endif

	MessageBox "Here Almalexia struck down upon the demon hordes of Ada'Soom Dir-Kamal with divine fury and all the splendor of stars. When her rage finally subsided, Kamal was no more."
	Set questionState to 0
	Return

endif


if ( questionState == 2 )

	Set button to GetButtonPressed

	if ( button == 1 )
		Set questionState to 0
		Return
	endif

	if ( button == 0 )

		if ( Player->GetItemCount "ingred_frost_salts_01"  > 0 )
			Player->RemoveItem "ingred_frost_salts_01" 1
			Set questionState to 3
			Return
		endif

		if ( Player->GetItemCount "T_IngMine_IceCrystal_01"  > 0 )
			Player->RemoveItem "T_IngMine_IceCrystal_01" 1
			Set questionState to 3
			Return
		endif


	endif
endif
	
if ( questionState == 3 )
	Cast "T_De_Res_AlmalexiaFury" Player
	MessageBox "The Gift of Almalexia's Divine Fury: Thank you, O Face-Snaked Queen, for teaching me how to strike down my enemies as you once struck down Ada'Soom Dir-Kamal."
	if ( doOnce == 0 )
		Journal TR_m4_TT_ShrineAlmaFury 10
		set TR_Pilgrimages to ( TR_Pilgrimages + 1 )
		set doOnce to 1
	endif
	Set questionState to 0
endif

End

Record: SCPT "tr_m4_rr_bodrumshrinescript" Flags:0x0000 ()

Begin TR_m4_RR_BodrumShrineScript

; Script on Activator TR_m4_RR_BodrumBattleShrine.
; This is the Shrine to the Battle of Bodrum, one of the Temple pilgrimage shrines.

short button
short questionState
short doOnce

if ( OnActivate == 1 )
	Set questionState to 1
	Return
endif

if ( questionState == 0 )
	Return
endif

if ( questionState == 1 )

	if ( Player->GetItemCount "iron spear" > 0 )
		MessageBox "Would you like to donate an iron spear and ask for a blessing?" "Yes" "No"
		Set questionState to 2
		Return
	endif

	if ( Player->GetItemCount "Iron Long Spear" > 0 )
		MessageBox "Would you like to donate an iron spear and ask for a blessing?" "Yes" "No"
		Set questionState to 2
		Return
	endif

	if ( Player->GetItemCount "TR_m3_iron spear_embedded_keep" > 0 )
		MessageBox "Would you like to donate an iron spear and ask for a blessing?" "Yes" "No"
		Set questionState to 2
		Return
	endif

	MessageBox "Here the forces led by Lord Vivec were victorious over the armies of Reman III. The raging waters of Pryai River washed away the taint of Cyrodiil, impaling them on a net of spears."
	Set questionState to 0
	Return

endif

if ( questionState == 2 )
	set button to GetButtonPressed

	if ( button == 0 )
		if ( Player->GetItemCount "iron spear" > 0 )
			Player->RemoveItem "iron spear" 1
		else
			if ( Player->GetItemCount "Iron Long Spear" > 0 )
				Player->RemoveItem "Iron Long Spear" 1
			else
				if ( Player->GetItemCount "TR_m3_iron spear_embedded_keep" > 0 )
					Player->RemoveItem "TR_m3_iron spear_embedded_keep" 1
				endif
			endif
		endif
		Cast "TR_m4_RR_BattleBodrumBlessing" Player
		MessageBox "Here the forces led by Lord Vivec were victorious over the armies of Reman III. The raging waters of Pryai River washed away the taint of Cyrodiil, impaling them on a net of spears. You are blessed with the power of those old days of glory."
		if ( doOnce == 0 )
			Journal TR_m4_TT_ShrineBodrum 10
			set TR_Pilgrimages to ( TR_Pilgrimages + 1 )
			set doOnce to 1
		endif
		Set questionState to 0
	endif

	if ( button == 1 )
		MessageBox "Here the forces led by Lord Vivec were victorious over the armies of Reman III. The raging waters of Pryai River washed away the taint of Cyrodiil, impaling them on a net of spears."
		Set questionState to 0
	endif

endif
	
End

Begin TR_m4_TT_DonationBoxScript

; Script on container TR_m4_And_Temple_Coffer for the Andothren Temple
; questline. This script is in charge of moving some Temple NPCs as well.

short doOnce
short checkGold
;global long TR_m4_TT_And_GoldCounter

if ( OnActivate )
	Activate
	if ( checkGold == 0 )
		set checkGold to 1
	endif
	Return
endif

if ( checkGold == 1 )
	if ( MenuMode == 0 )
		set checkGold to 0
		set TR_m4_TT_And_GoldCounter to ( getitemcount gold_001 )
;		MessageBox "Gold amount %G" TR_m4_TT_And_GoldCounter
	endif

		TR_m4_TT_Ravur_Othravel->PositionCell 5700 -130000 200 2500 Andothren
		TR_m4_TT_Ravur_Othravel->AIWander 0 0 0 0
		set doOnce to 1
	endif
elseif ( doOnce == 1 )
	if ( GetJournalIndex TR_m4_TT_KitchenSupplies >= 90 )
		TR_m4_TT_Ravur_Othravel->PositionCell 3940 4349 14753 15000 "Andothren, Temple"
		TR_m4_TT_Ravur_Othravel->AIWander 0, 0, 5, 0, 40, 0, 10, 0, 5, 5, 25, 5
		TR_m4_TT_Ravur_Othravel->Set controlQ to 5
		set doOnce to 2
	endif
elseif ( doOnce == 2 )
	if ( GetJournalIndex TR_m4_TT_TroublesomeOrc > 20 )
		if ( CellChanged )
			TR_m4_TT_Tevuren_Galdar->PositionCell -380 522 -255 1920 "Sinramen Monastery"
			TR_m4_TT_Tevuren_Galdar->AIWander 0 0 0 25 10 0 10 20 5 10 20 0
			set doOnce to 3
		endif
	endif
elseif ( doOnce == 3 )
	if ( GetJournalIndex TR_m4_TT_Forgiveness >= 100 )
		if ( CellChanged )
			set doOnce to 4
			SetPos X 3772.126
			SetPos Y 4014.329
			SetPos Z 14600.051
			SetAngle Z 0
		endif
	endif
elseif ( doOnce == 4 )
	if ( TR_m4_TT_AndothrenFinale )
		set doOnce to 5
		PositionCell 4852.568 3661.374 15499.300 5502 "Omaynis, Ulmon Vathri's House"
	endif

Record: SCPT "tr_m4_tt_felani_vathri_sc" Flags:0x0000 ()
  SCHD: ID:TR_m4_TT_Felani_Vathri_sc  Num_Shorts:6  Num_Longs:3  Num_Floats:0  Data_Size:1664  Local_Var_Size:73
  SCVR: Script_Variables: TR_Map,control,controlQ,NoLore,T_Local_NPC,T_Local_NoLore,posX,posY,posZ
  SCDT: Bytecode: (compiled script code)
  SCTX: Script_Text:
Begin TR_m4_TT_Felani_Vathri_sc

; Script on NPC TR_m4_TT_Felani_Vathri (Ulmon's daughter)
; for Andothren Temple quest TR_m4_TT_LastWillAndTestament.

short TR_Map
short control
short controlQ
short NoLore
short T_Local_NPC
short T_Local_NoLore
long posX
long posY
long posZ

; Enable only from the quest onwards.

if ( GetJournalIndex TR_m4_TT_LastWillAndTestament < 20 )
	if ( GetDisabled == 0 )
		Disable
	endif
	Return
elseif ( GetJournalIndex TR_m4_TT_LastWillAndTestament >= 20 )
	if ( GetDisabled == 1 )
		Enable
	endif
endif

if ( control == 0 )
	if ( GetDistance player < 400 )
		set control to 1
		Say "TR\Vo\TR_DeF_Cry.mp3" "[Soft weeping.]"
	endif
endif

if ( controlQ == 1 )
	; Felani is following the player to the Temple, yet outside the Temple.
	; if ( CellChanged )
	; Commented this out, since it seems to sometimes fail to fire
	; (maybe because Felani appears in the Temple later than the
	; player?). -- arvisrend
		if ( GetPCCell "Andothren, Temple" )
			PositionCell 3592 4184 14784 14034 "Andothren, Temple"
			AIFollow player 0 0 0 0
			if ( GetDeadCount TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus == 0 )
				TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus->PositionCell 3592 4320 14784 17820 "Andothren, Temple"
				TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus->AIFollow TR_m4_TT_Felani_Vathri 0 0 0 0
			endif
			set controlQ to 2
		endif
	; endif
elseif ( controlQ == 2 )
	; Felani is following the player inside the Andothren Temple.
	; Don't follow the player out of the Temple!
	; if ( CellChanged )
		if ( GetPCCell "Andothren, Temple" != 1 )
			PositionCell 3592 4184 14784 14034 "Andothren, Temple"
			AIFollow player 0 0 0 0
			if ( GetDeadCount TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus == 0 )
				TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus->PositionCell 3592 4320 14784 17820 "Andothren, Temple"
				TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus->AIFollow TR_m4_TT_Felani_Vathri 0 0 0 0
			endif
			return
		endif
	; endif
	if ( GetPos Z < 14352 )
		if ( GetDistance TR_m4_TT_Ulmon_Dead < 800 )
			Journal TR_m4_TT_LastWillAndTestament 30
			set controlQ to 3
			set TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus.controlQ to 3
			AITravel 4016 4160 14016
			if ( GetDeadCount TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus == 0 )
				TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus->AITravel 4056 4256 14016
			endif
		endif
	endif
elseif ( controlQ == 3 )
	if ( GetAIPackageDone )
		set controlQ to 4
		AIWander 0 0 0 10 20 0 30 20 0 0 20 0
		Face 4148 3980
	endif
elseif ( controlQ == 5 )
	if ( GetInterior == 0 )
		if ( GetDistance player > 500 )
			;do nothing
		elseif ( GetPCCell "Andothren" )
			; move marja
			if ( GetDeadCount TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus == 0 )
				TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus->PositionCell 2498 -132190 500 0 "Andothren"
				TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus->AITravel 5370 -132967 74
				set TR_m4_TT_Marja_Iannus.controlQ to 5
			endif
			PositionCell 2630 -132160 500 0 "Andothren"
			Say "Vo\D\F\Flw_DF003.mp3" "Thank you."
			Journal TR_m4_TT_LastWillAndTestament 45
			AITravel 5267 -132962 72
			set controlQ to 9
			Return
			endif
		endif
	endif
elseif ( controlQ <= 7 )
	if ( controlQ >= 6 )
		if ( controlQ == 6 )
			if ( GetAIPackageDone )
				set controlQ to 7
				AIWander 0 0 0 10 20 0 30 20 0 0 20 0
			endif
		endif
		if ( CellChanged )
			set controlQ to 8
			PositionCell 3682 3960 14214 8694 "Andothren, The Dancing Cup"
			AIWander 0 0 0 10 20 0 30 20 0 0 20 0
		endif
	endif
elseif ( controlQ == 9 )
	; bounceback!
	set controlQ to 6
endif

if ( TR_Map )
	return
endif

set TR_Map to 4

End

		if ( TR_m4_TT_AndothrenFinale == 0 )

		endif

		if ( TR_m4_TT_AndothrenFinale )
			Enable
		endif
	endif

		if ( GetPos Y == 0 )
			if ( GetPos Z == 0 )

				set doOnce to -1
				Return
			endif
		endif
	endif
	set doOnce to 1
endif

End

Begin TR_m4_TT_ShrineOlmsReflct_sc

; Script on activator TR_m4_TT_ShrineOlmsReflct, the Shrine of St. Olms' Reflection
; (an Andothren Temple pilgrimage site).

short state
short localDaysPassed
short localHour
short doOnce

if ( OnActivate == 1 )
	if ( state == 0 )
		set state to 1
		set localDaysPassed to DaysPassed
		set localHour to GameHour
	endif
	if ( state <= 1 )
		MessageBox "At the end of his days, Saint Olms meditated on this rock for a day and a night. He beheld the starry skies of Lady Almalexia, the swelling sea of Lord Sotha Sil, and all he had helped Lord Vivec build."
	else
		MessageBox "The Blessing of a Heart at Peace: As the good Saint Olms reflected on his life and service, he found himself at ease. No deed remained undone, no words left unsaid, and he went into the tomb of his Fathers without fear or remorse."
		Cast TR_m4_TT_ShrineOlmsRefl_sp player
		if ( doOnce == 0 )
			Journal TR_m4_TT_ShrineOlmsRest 10
			set TR_Pilgrimages to ( TR_Pilgrimages + 1 )
			set doOnce to 1
		endif
		set state to 0
	endif
endif

if ( state == 1 )
	if ( GetDistance player > 300 )
		set state to 0
		Return
	endif
	if ( DaysPassed == ( localDaysPassed + 1 ) )
		if ( localHour <= GameHour )
			set state to 2
		endif
	elseif ( DaysPassed > ( localDaysPassed + 1 ) )
		set state to 2
	endif

Record: SCPT "tr_m4_tt_tribunalshrine" Flags:0x0000 ()
  SCHD: ID:TR_m4_TT_TribunalShrine  Num_Shorts:4  Num_Longs:0  Num_Floats:0  Data_Size:2282  Local_Var_Size:37
  SCVR: Script_Variables: button,donation,QuestionState,doOnce
  SCDT: Bytecode: (compiled script code)
  SCTX: Script_Text:
Begin TR_m4_TT_TribunalShrine

; Script on activator TR_m4_And_Temple_Shrine, a shrine in the Andothren Temple.
; Besides the usual functions of a shrine, this handles some NPC moving for the
; Andothren Temple questline.



;Cure Common Disease [and Cure Common Disease Other] do not currently work through scripts; reported as a bug
short button
short donation
short QuestionState
short doOnce

if ( CellChanged )
	if ( doOnce == 0 )
		if ( GetJournalIndex TR_m4_TT_LastWillAndTestament == 200 )
			set doOnce to 1	;both dead, do nothing
		elseif ( GetJournalIndex TR_m4_TT_LastWillAndTestament_b > 80 )
			set doOnce to 1
			PositionCell 4272 4384 15103.7 16200 "Andothren, Temple"
;			TR_m4_And_Temple_Triolith->Disable
			TR_m4_TT_Ravur_Othravel->PositionCell 4276 4470 15120 6600 "Andothren, Temple"
			TR_m4_TT_Ravur_Othravel->AIWander 0, 0, 5, 0, 40, 0, 10, 0, 5, 5, 25, 5
		elseif ( GetJournalIndex TR_m4_TT_LastWillAndTestament_c >= 80 )
			set doOnce to 1
			TR_m4_TT_Nalvs_Andolin->PositionCell 4276 4470 15120 6600 "Andothren, Temple"
			TR_m4_TT_Nalvs_Andolin->AIWander 0 0 5 20 20 20 0 10 10 20 0
		endif
	endif
endif

if ( menumode == 1 )
	return
endif

if ( OnActivate == 0 )
	if ( QuestionState == 0 )
		Return
	endif
endif

;set donation amount
if ( player->GetPCRank "Temple" >= 2 )			;member of rank 2 or above
	Set donation to 0
elseif ( player->GetPCRank "Temple" >= 0 )		;member below rank 2
	Set donation to 5
else																;not a member
	Set donation to 35
endif

if ( Player->GetItemCount Gold_001 < donation )
	MessageBox "You do not have enough gold to make a donation." "OK"
	Return
endif

if ( QuestionState == 0 )
	MessageBox "Would you like to make a donation of %.0f and receive a blessing?" donation "Yes" "No"
	set QuestionState to 10
endif

;Ask second question 
if ( QuestionState == 10 )

	Set button to GetButtonPressed

	if ( button == 0 )
		MessageBox "What blessing do you ask for?" "Cure Disease" "Cure Blight" "Cure Poison" "Lady's Grace" "Soul of Sotha Sil" "Vivec's Mystery" "Almsivi Restoration"
		set QuestionState to 20
	elseif ( button == 1 )
		set QuestionState to 0
	endif

	Return

endif

;perform cure or give message
if ( QuestionState == 20 )
	
	Set button to GetButtonPressed

	if ( button == 0 )
		if ( Player->GetCommonDisease == 1 )
			Cast "Cure Common Disease Other" Player
			if ( donation == 35 )
				Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 35
			elseif ( donation == 5 )
				Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 5
			endif
		else
			MessageBox "You are not afflicted with a common disease." "OK"
		endif
		Set QuestionState to 0
	endif
	
	if ( button == 1 )
		if ( Player->GetBlightDisease == 1 )
			Cast "Cure Blight Disease" Player
			if ( donation == 35 )
				Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 35
			elseif ( donation == 5 )
				Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 5
			endif
		else
			MessageBox "You are not afflicted with a blight disease." "OK"
		endif
		Set QuestionState to 0
	endif

	if ( button == 2 )
		if ( Player->GetEffect sEffectPoison == 1 )				;check for poison effect on player
			Cast "Cure Poison Touch" Player
			if ( donation == 35 )
				Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 35
			elseif ( donation == 5 )
				Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 5
			endif
		else
			MessageBox "You are not poisoned." "OK"
		endif
		Set QuestionState to 0
	endif
	
	if ( button == 3 )
		Cast "Lady's Grace shrine" Player					;Fortify Endurance 5
		if ( donation == 35 )
			Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 35
		elseif ( donation == 5 )
			Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 5
		endif
		Set QuestionState to 0
	endif

	if ( button == 4 )
		Cast "Soul of Sotha Sil" Player					;Fortify Magicka 5
		if ( donation == 35 )
			Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 35
		elseif ( donation == 5 )
			Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 5
		endif
		Set QuestionState to 0
	endif


	if ( button == 5 )
		Cast "Vivec's Mystery" Player					;Fortify Luck 10
		if ( donation == 25 )
			Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 25
		elseif ( donation == 5 )
			Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 5
		endif
		Set QuestionState to 0
	endif


	if ( button == 6 )
		Cast "Almsivi Restoration" Player					;restore eight attributes
		Cast "Almsivi Restore Fighter" Player					;restore eight fighter skills
		Cast "Almsivi Restore Mage" Player					;restore eight mage skills
		Cast "Almsivi Restore Stealth" Player					;restore eight stealth skills
		Cast "Almsivi Restore Other" Player					;restore three other skills
		if ( donation == 25 )
			Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 25
		elseif ( donation == 5 )
			Player->RemoveItem Gold_001 5
		endif
		Set QuestionState to 0
	endif

endif

End

Record: SCPT "tr_rothroryn_monastery_script" Flags:0x0000 ()
  SCHD: ID:TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_Script  Num_Shorts:3  Num_Longs:0  Num_Floats:0  Data_Size:397  Local_Var_Size:33
  SCVR: Script_Variables: lastHealth,openDoor,finishedMove
  SCDT: Bytecode: (compiled script code)
  SCTX: Script_Text:
begin TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_Script

; Script on activator TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_DoorAct.

short lastHealth
short openDoor
short finishedMove

if ( MenuMode == 1 )
	return
endif

if ( finishedMove == 1 )
	if ( cellChanged )
		; Make sure the secret passage remains open, even if the
		; cell gets recycled.
		TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_Wall01->SetPos, Z, 0
		TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_Wall02->SetPos, Z, 0
	endif
	return
endif

if ( openDoor == 1 )
	TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_Wall01->MoveWorld, Y, 5
	TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_Wall02->MoveWorld, Y, 5
	if ( ( TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_Wall01->GetPos, Y ) >= 3360 )
		set openDoor to 0
		set finishedMove to 1
	endif
	return
endif

if ( GetDistance, player <= 200 )
	if ( ( player->GetHealth ) < lastHealth )
		set openDoor to 1
		PlaySound3D "Door Stone Open" 
	endif
	set lastHealth to ( player->GetHealth )
else
	set lastHealth to 0
endif

end TR_RothRoryn_Monastery_Script
